### Mount points

| Name | Accepts | Params | apply | append | place | detach | sync | replay | prefer_sync |
|------|---------|--------|-------|--------|-------|--------|------|--------|-------------|
| `menu_bar` | `pyrolyze.backends.dearpygui.items.DpgMenuBarItem` | — | attach_menu_bar | — | — | — | — | `NONE` | `True` |
| `standard` | `pyrolyze.backends.dearpygui.items.DpgItem` | — | — | — | — | — | sync_children | `ANCHOR_BEFORE` | `True` |

### Default child attachment

- `default_child_mount_point_name`: `'standard'`
- `default_attach_mount_point_names`: `('menu_bar', 'standard')`
